══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  SECTION 3 — CLAUDE ANALYSIS NOTES
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

  This section is written for Claude to read at the start of a research session.
  It summarises what happened, what looks suspicious, and what to try next.
  All recommendations reference the GRA document set (reconstruction_algorithms.md,
  genealogical_constraints.md) where relevant.


  ── Issues detected
  ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  ISSUE 1:
    High-frequency surnames detected: 'graham' (220), 'cassidy' (152),
    'wray' (148), 'gallagher' (118), 'travers' (92). In a small townland
    community, dominant surnames create many same-surname candidate
    pairs. Without Splink term-frequency (TF) adjustment, a surname match
    carries the same discriminating weight regardless of frequency,
    inflating match probabilities for ambiguous pairs
    (reconstruction_algorithms.md §4.4).

  ISSUE 2:
    214 pairs scored in [0.80–0.85), just below the auto-commit threshold
    of 0.85. These were queued as proposals rather than committed. If
    manual review of these proposals shows they are mostly correct
    linkages, the threshold may be conservatively high for this dataset.
    If they are mostly incorrect, the model needs more training data.

  ISSUE 3:
    104 pairs scored in [0.30–0.35), just above the suppression floor.
    These low-confidence proposals may represent transcription-damaged
    records or extended-family members with similar names. They warrant
    careful review and are likely flag candidates rather than accepts.


  ── What looks good
  ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  ✓ Feature matrix (3167 persons across 3 census sources) is adequate for
  Splink EM parameter estimation.
  ✓ Birth year null rate: 2% — good feature coverage.
  ✓ Place null rate: 0% — most persons have a resolved townland.
  ✓ 408 persons auto-committed at mean score 0.963.
  ✓ 1942 pairs proposed for researcher review.
  ✓ Place match rate among merged pairs: 99% — good spatial coherence.
  Merges are consistent with GC22 geographical coherence.
  ✓ All merged pairs have birth year delta ≤ 5 years (max: 4). Consistent
  with GC03 census age drift tolerances.

  ── Recommended actions
  ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  ACTION 1:
    Enable Splink term-frequency adjustment for surname_norm. In
    _build_settings(), configure the JaroWinklerAtThresholds comparison
    for surname_norm with term_frequency_adjustments=True. The frequency
    table is computed automatically from the feature DataFrame by
    Splink's EM training.

  ACTION 2:
    In the update-knowledge session, review the 214 near-commit proposals
    first. If ≥80% are correct, consider lowering AUTO_COMMIT_THRESHOLD
    to 0.82 on a trial basis. Document the decision in ROADMAP.md.
